Cejtlin's Old Church Slavonic Dictionary

Tips:

  • If you don't have Old Cyrillic letters on your keyboard, use the input buttons to the right.
  • Press the Cyrillic ё key instead of clicking to put the cursor in the search box.
  • Press the enter key in the search box to open the dictionary entry of the word which is highlighted in the list on the left.
  • The hyphen character ('-') is used at the start of each dictionary entry title; use it to match the beginning of a word.
  • The underscore character ('_') is used at the end of each word in the dictionary entry titles.
  • Install the Buky Vede font from here to make the page look cool.
  • While the cursor is in the search box and a word is highlighted in the list on the left, you can use the up & down arrow keys to navigate to the previous/next word.

If you find any errors, please write to me at
j.walker@cantab.net
